! ============ !
! Proper nouns !
! ============ !

! Note: the final non-sámi consonants: 
!          b  d  g  h  m  n  p  z
! write as b3 d3 g3 h3 m3 n3 p3 z3

! j that shall always be j (also in V_C) is written j3, as eg. in Ajja (Aj3ja) 

! Table of content
! ----------------
! Continuation lexica
! Personal names
!  First names
!  Surnames
! Place names
! ----------------

! Aspell lexica
! =============

! This is a lexicon to be used with aspell spell checker only.
! Target is to use as many sublexicons as possible with as many variables 
! as possible to create aspell affix file.

LEXICON AspellProp
Aspell LONDON ;
Spelle ACCRA ;
! MARJA-plc & MARJA use same affixes as GOAHTI
Cbern:Cbern3 BERN ;		! Same as BLIND
Duominen:Duomi C-FI-NEN ;
Blondon:Blondon3 LONDON ;		! VUOLAB goes here
ENYSTØ NYSTØ ;
! PLACE-DIM is same as DIMINC
Ejeakkit:Ejeaggi ALEUHTAT ;

! Continuation lexica
! ===================

! Some of the entries point to continuation lexica in the sme-lex.txt
! file, such as GOAHTI. This implies that names have the same inflection as
! ordinary nouns, which is probably not true. These lexica must thus be re-
! vised as soon as the lexica for names become more accurate.

! Continuation lexica for personal names
! --------------------------------------

! Vowel final names
! - - - - - - - - -

LEXICON ACCRA-ani
 +N+Prop+Ani: ACCRADECL ; 

LEXICON ACCRA-obj
 +N+Prop+Obj: ACCRADECL ; 
 
LEXICON ACCRA-org
 +N+Prop+Org: ACCRADECL ; 
 
LEXICON ACCRA-mal
 +N+Prop+Mal:  ACCRADECL ; 
 +N+Prop+Mal+Sg+Attr:@U.Cap.Obl@ # ; ! it shall be used in cases like Konrad Nielsenii
 
LEXICON ACCRA-fem
 +N+Prop+Fem:  ACCRADECL ; 
 +N+Prop+Fem+Sg+Attr:@U.Cap.Obl@ # ; ! it shall be used in cases like Konrad Nielsenii
 
LEXICON ACCRA-malfem
 +N+Prop+Fem:  ACCRADECL ; 
 +N+Prop+Mal:  ACCRADECL ; 
 +N+Prop+Fem+Sg+Attr:@U.Cap.Obl@ # ; ! it shall be used in cases like Konrad Nielsenii
 +N+Prop+Mal+Sg+Attr:@U.Cap.Obl@ # ; ! it shall be used in cases like Konrad Nielsenii

LEXICON ACCRA-sur
 +N+Prop+Sur: ACCRADECL ;
 +N+Prop+Sur+Sg+Attr:@U.Cap.Obl@ # ; ! it shall be used in cases like Konrad Nielsenii
 
LEXICON ACCRA-plc ! Place names
 +N+Prop+Plc:  ACCRADECL ;

LEXICON ACCRA-surplc ! Names that are both surnames and place names
 +N+Prop+Sur: ACCRADECL ;
 +N+Prop+Sur+Sg+Attr:@U.Cap.Obl@ # ; ! it shall be used in cases like Konrad Nielsenii
 +N+Prop+Plc: ACCRADECL ;

LEXICON ACCRA ! Vowel-final names without Gradation and Ill change
 +N+Prop: ACCRADECL ;

LEXICON ACCRADECL
! These sublexica are irrelevant for ACCRA, but added
! for the sake of the lexicon MARJA
 ACCRA-DC ;
 @U.Cap.Obl@ ACCRA-I ;		! correct suffixes
 @U.Cap.Obl@ ACCRA-OBL ;
 @U.Cap.Obl@ ACCRA-IICASE ;
 @U.Cap.Obl@ DenominalAdjsC ; !^C^

 +Comp+Sg+Nom:X4b K ;
 +Comp+Sg+Gen:X4bu K ;
 +Comp+Sg+Gen:X4b K ;
 +Comp+Sg+Acc:X4bu K ;
 +Comp+Sg+Acc:X4b K ;

 +Sg+Ill:j K ;

LEXICON ACCRA-OBL
 +Sg+Gen: K ;
 +Sg+Gen:# R ; ! for placenames  !^C^

 +Sg+Loc:s K ;
 +Sg+Com:jn K ;
 +Pl+Nom:t K ;

 +Pl+Gen:jd K ;
 +Pl+Acc:jd K ;
 +Pl+Ill:jde K ;
 +Pl+Loc:jn K ;
 +Pl+Com:jgujn K ;

! Vowel-final names where the final vowel carries
! primary or secondary stress. Monosyllables and
! Scandinavian stressed compounds in -V belong here.

LEXICON NYSTØ-fem
 +N+Prop+Fem: NYSTØDECL ;
 +N+Prop+Fem+Sg+Attr:@U.Cap.Obl@ # ; ! it shall be used in cases like Konrad Nielsenii

LEXICON NYSTØ-mal
 +N+Prop+Mal:  NYSTØDECL ;
 +N+Prop+Mal+Sg+Attr:@U.Cap.Obl@ # ; ! it shall be used in cases like Konrad Nielsenii

LEXICON NYSTØ-obj
 +N+Prop+Obj:  NYSTØDECL ;

LEXICON NYSTØ-org
 +N+Prop+Org:  NYSTØDECL ;

LEXICON NYSTØ-sur
 +N+Prop+Sur:  NYSTØDECL ;
 +N+Prop+Sur+Sg+Attr:@U.Cap.Obl@ # ; ! it shall be used in cases like Konrad Nielsenii

LEXICON NYSTØ-surplc
 +N+Prop+Sur:  NYSTØDECL ;
 +N+Prop+Sur+Sg+Attr:@U.Cap.Obl@ # ; ! it shall be used in cases like Konrad Nielsenii
 +N+Prop+Plc:  NYSTØDECL ;

LEXICON NYSTØ-plc ! Place names
 +N+Prop+Plc:  NYSTØDECL ;

LEXICON NYSTØ ! Vowel-final, heavy syll
 +N+Prop: NYSTØDECL ;
 
LEXICON NYSTØDECL
 @U.Cap.Obl@ NYSTØ-OBL ;
 @U.Cap.Opt@ NYSTØ-DC ; !^C^

LEXICON NYSTØ-OBL 
 +Sg+Nom: K ;	
 +Sg+Nom: R ;			!^C^
 +Sg+Loc:%:s K ; ! Nystø:s
 +Sg+Gen#:a# R ; ! for placenames !^C^
 NYOBL ;
 :%: NYOBL ; ! to NYOBL, optional delimiter marks. sub?
 :%- NYOBL ;  
 :'1 NYOBL ; 

LEXICON NYSTØ-DC						!^C^
 +laš:lažž DEARVVASLAS ;		!^C^

LEXICON NYOBL
 +Sg+Gen:a K ;
 +Sg+Acc:a K ;
 +Sg+Ill:aj K ;
 +Sg+Loc:as K ;
 +Sg+Com:ajn K ;
 +Ess:an K ;
 +Pl+Nom:at K ;
 +Pl+Gen:ajd K ;
 +Pl+Acc:ajd K ;
 +Pl+Ill:ajde K ;
 +Pl+Loc:ajn K ;
 +Pl+Com:ajgujn K ;

LEXICON PLACE-DIM-OBL
 +Sg+Nom: K ;
 +Sg+Nom:X7 R ;	!^C^
 +Ess:in K ;
 +Sg+Gen:a K ;
 +Sg+Gen: K ;
 +Sg+Gen:a R ; !^C^ compound also for these
 +Sg+Gen: R ;  !^C^ compound also for these
 +Sg+Acc:a K ;
 +Sg+Acc: K ;
 +Pl+Nom:at K ;
 :i PLACE-DIM-i ;

LEXICON PLACE-DIM-i
 +Sg+Ill:j K ;
 +Sg+Loc:s K ;
 +Sg+Com:jn K ;

 +Pl+Acc:jd K ;
 +Pl+Ill:jdda K ;
 +Pl+Loc:jn K ;
 +Pl+Com:jgujn K ;

LEXICON C-FI-NEN-sur
! For Finnish surnames. Itkonen.
 +N+Prop+Sur: C-FI-NENDECL ;

LEXICON C-FI-NEN-plc
! For Finnish placenames with ending -nen. Kaustinen.
 +N+Prop+Plc: C-FI-NENDECL ;

LEXICON C-FI-NEN-surplc
! For Finnish names with ending -nen that are used both surnames and placenames. Huittinen.
 +N+Prop+Sur: C-FI-NENDECL ;

! Finnish Itkonen, lexicon for Finnish nen-names

LEXICON C-FI-NEN
 +N+Prop: C-FI-NENDECL ;

LEXICON C-FI-NENDECL  ! Finnish names
 :s FI-S ;            ! In Finland, they are declined with
                      ! Itkosa as the oblique stem.
 :nen3 LONDON ;       ! In Norway, they are declined as CNAME
                      ! with ordinary genitive Itkonena

! Finnish Itkosa
LEXICON FI-S
 @U.Cap.Obl@ FI-S-OBL ;
 @U.Cap.Opt@ FI-S-DC ; !^C^

 +Pl+Acc:ijd K ;
 +Pl+Ill:ijdda K ;
 +Pl+Loc:ijn K ;
 +Pl+Com:ijgujn K ;

LEXICON FI-S-DC						!^C^
 +laš:lažž DEARVVASLAS ;		!^C^
